### [103] [Open Effective Field Theory and the Physics of Cosmological Collider Signals](https://arxiv.org/abs/2512.07941)
*Thomas Colas,Zhehan Qin,Xi Tong*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文通过开放有效场论框架研究宇宙学对撞机信号的起源，发现三谱可分解为局域与非局域部分，分别源于有效理论的幺正部分和随机噪声部分，并将非局域信号与熵产生及量子态混合度联系起来。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解宇宙学对撞机信号的物理起源，特别是其局域与非局域成分的微观机制及其与量子开放系统性质（如耗散、噪声、熵产）的关联。

Method: 采用开有效场论框架，将重场传播子在Keldysh基下分解，对重标量场做单交换近似，导出轻标量场的单场有效理论，区分幺正项与非幺正（耗散与随机）项，并分析其动量依赖性与可观测量的关系。

Result: 三谱清晰分裂为局域（来自幺正有效作用）和非局域（源自随机噪声）两部分；有效理论系数虽具运动学非解析性，但在质量等级展开下可软化；非局域信号被证明与熵产生及量子态混合度直接相关。

Conclusion: 宇宙学对撞机的非局域信号本质上是量子开放系统特性的体现，其观测可作为原初量子态非纯度的探针，为早期宇宙量子退相干提供新观测窗口。

Abstract: We examine the origin of the cosmological collider signal using the framework of open effective field theories. Focusing on the single exchange of a massive scalar field, we demonstrate that the trispectrum splits cleanly into its local and non-local components once the heavy-field propagators are decomposed in the Keldysh basis. Integrating out the massive degree of freedom yields a single-field effective field theory for the light scalar that necessarily contains both unitary operators and non-unitary contributions associated with dissipation and stochastic noise. We show that the leading local signal in parity-preserving theories arises from the unitary part of this effective field theory, whereas the non-local signal is intrinsically associated with its stochastic sector. The effective field theory coefficients themselves are a priori non-analytic in the external kinematics; however, this non-analyticity can be softened when a scale hierarchy - such as the heavy-mass expansion - is imposed, up to spurious contributions that ultimately cancel in observables. Finally, we establish a connection between the cosmological collider signal and entropy production, linking the observable non-local signal to intrinsic properties of the quantum state, including its degree of mixedness.

</details>

Abstract: Recent advances in holography and quantum gravity have shown that CFTs with classical gravity duals can implement nonlocal quantum computation protocols that appear local from the bulk perspective. Specifically, standard Lorentzian threads cannot account for the negativity of `mutual complexity' and its higher-partite generalizations. We then prove that when the kinematic coefficients in both expansion steps satisfy the one-loop consistency conditions, the EYM integrand is finally expanded as a combination of YM integrands with quadratic propagators. The coefficients in this expansion formula coincide exactly with those in the expansion formula for YMS integrands. This correspondence highlights a shared kinematic structure, providing the proper foundation for constructing BCJ numerators in both YMS and EYM theories at one loop.

Abstract: We investigate the Einstein-Hilbert black brane solution in four-dimensional Anti-de Sitter (AdS) spacetime supplemented by a quadratic Ricci scalar term $q L^2 R^2$, where $q$ is a dimensionless coupling constant and $L$ is the AdS radius. The shear viscosity to entropy density ratio, $\fracη{s}$, is calculated holographically, and deviations from the universal Kovtun-Son-Starinets (KSS) bound are analyzed. Our results indicate that $\fracη{s} = \frac{1}{4π}(1 - 24q)$, demonstrating that the ratio falls below the conjectured lower limit for positive $q$, while it respects the bound for negative $q$. We confirm that our solutions smoothly reduce to the standard Einstein-Hilbert case when $q \to 0$, consistent with expectations. The physical implications of violating the KSS bound are discussed in depth, particularly regarding stability, causality, and the strongly coupled nature of the dual field theory. These findings provide valuable insights into the influence of higher curvature terms on holographic transport properties.

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解极端黑洞微观结构及其与超引力解的对应关系，特别是探索介于黑洞与非黑洞（如超紧凑天体）之间的过渡区域，以及相关相变机制。

Method: 采用基于brane有效作用量的方法，在branes轻微分离的极限下构造新的BPS超引力解；分析弦探针响应、几何结构（如AdS2喉部）、集体模式，并将解与已知superstratum几何比较；研究源合并极限下的半经典失效与相变行为。

Result: 获得一大类由手性波形参数化的BPS解；发现其中存在大量具有深AdS2喉部的超紧凑天体；识别出类Schwarzian的集体动力学模式；揭示五膜退禁闭与Hawking-Page相变的全息对应。

Conclusion: 这类解提供了黑洞微观结构的新视角，表明极端黑洞可视为五膜源凝聚相，其前黑洞性质由源分离尺度调控；半经典失效标志从‘星’到‘洞’的相变临界点，强化了AdS/CFT中相变与量子引力效应的联系。

Abstract: We construct a large new class of BPS supergravity solutions parametrized by arbitrary chiral wave profiles on fundamental string and Neveu-Schwarz fivebrane sources. The effective action approach we employ describes the regime where the brane sources are slightly separated. String probes see these backgrounds as smooth and effectively capped off at the scale of that separation. Within the space of solutions is a large ensemble of ultracompact objects exhibiting many of the features of extremal BTZ black holes, in particular having a deep $AdS_2$ throat. We present the details of solutions with circular source profiles, and compare them to known superstratum geometries. The separation of the sources makes them structurally more like BPS fivebrane stars than like extremal black hole microstates. When evaluated on the supergravity background, the brane effective action governs (chaotic) near-BPS dynamics, and exhibits a collective mode analogous to the Schwarzian mode of $AdS_2$ black holes. Finally, we discuss the approach to the black hole phase as the sources coalesce, in which the semiclassical approximation breaks down due to the appearance of light D-brane excitations; this bulk realization of the fivebrane deconfinement transition connects directly to the Hawking-Page transition.

</details>


### [114] [Vacuum Energy and Topological Mass in Interacting Elko and Scalar Field Theories](https://arxiv.org/abs/2512.08750)
*A. J. D. Farias Junior,A. Smirnov,Herondy F. Santana Mota,E. R. Bezerra de Mello*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文研究了在Dirichlet边界条件下，四维空间中Elko费米场与实标量场相互作用系统的Casimir效应，计算了真空能量密度及其耦合常数的一阶修正，并分别分析了由边界条件诱导的拓扑质量修正。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 分析Elko费米场与实标量场在受限几何（平行板）下的量子真空效应，特别是Casimir效应及其对场质量的影响。

Method: 采用基于路径积分的量子场论有效势方法，结合Dirichlet边界条件，计算真空能量密度、耦合常数的一阶修正及各场的拓扑质量修正。

Result: 得到了真空能量密度及其一阶耦合修正；导出了依赖于耦合常数的Elko场和标量场各自的拓扑质量修正。

Conclusion: 边界条件不仅引发Casimir效应，还通过量子修正赋予Elko和标量场非零拓扑质量，揭示了该系统中几何约束与相互作用的协同物理效应。

Abstract: In this paper, we consider a four-dimensional system composed of a mass-dimension-one fermionic field, also known as Elko, interacting with a real scalar field. Our main objective is to analyze the Casimir effects associated with this system, assuming that both the Elko and scalar fields satisfy Dirichlet boundary conditions on two large parallel plates separated by a distance $L$. In this scenario, we calculate the vacuum energy density and its first-order correction in the coupling constants of the theory. Additionally, we consider the mass correction for each field separately, namely the topological mass that arises from the boundary conditions imposed on the fields and which also depends on the coupling constants. To develop this analysis, we use the mathematical formalism known as the effective potential, expressed as a path integral in quantum field theory.

### [115] [Exact $S$-duality Map for Rigid Surface Operators](https://arxiv.org/abs/2512.08801)
*Chuanzhong Li,Xiaoman Luo,Bao Shou*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种直接、自然且精确的S对偶映射，用于四维规范理论中的刚性面算符，通过在定义面算符的两个分拆之间移动最长行并增减一个方格来实现，从而自然包含非刚性面算符，解决了长期存在的‘不匹配问题’。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 解决刚性面算符在S对偶下因不变量相同或数量不匹配（即‘不匹配问题’）而导致对偶关系难以确定的问题，并拓展对偶映射至更广范围。

Method: 通过在表征面算符的一对分拆之间移动最长行，并添加或删除一个方格以保持总方格数守恒，构造一种新的S对偶映射；该方法自然引入非刚性面算符。

Result: 提出了适用于任意秩规范群的普适S对偶映射，成功解决不匹配问题，并澄清了领域内多个长期未解的疑难。

Conclusion: 刚性面算符的S对偶需超越纯刚性分类，引入非刚性结构；所提出的映射是自然、精确且普适的，为理解四维规范理论的非微扰结构提供了新工具。

Abstract: Surface operators in four-dimensional gauge theories are two-dimensional defects, serving as natural generalizations of Wilson lines and 't Hooft line operators. They act as ideal probes for exploring the non-perturbative structure of the theory. Rigid surface operators are a specific class of surface operators characterized by the absence of continuous deformation parameters. It is expected that a closed $S$-duality map should exist among these rigid operators. While progress has been made on specific examples or subclasses by leveraging invariants and empirical conjectures, a complete picture remains elusive.
  A significant challenge arises when multiple rigid surface operators share identical invariants, making the determination of $S$-duality relations difficult. More critically, a mismatch exists in the number of rigid surface operators between dual theories when classified by invariants; this is referred to as the \textit{mismatch problem}. This discrepancy suggests the necessity of extending the scope of consideration beyond strictly rigid operators.
  In this paper, we propose a direct, natural, and precise $S$-duality map for rigid surface operators.
  Our map is realized by moving the longest row in the pair of partitions defining a surface operator from one factor to the other, with an additional box appended or deleted to balance the total number of boxes.
  This mapping naturally incorporates non-rigid surface operators, thereby resolving the mismatch problem. The proposed map is applicable to gauge groups of all ranks and clarifies several long-standing puzzles in the field.

</details>


### [116] [The Strong-$CP$ Problem and its Gauge Axion solution as Evidence for Fundamental Strings](https://arxiv.org/abs/2512.08834)
*Gia Dvali,Lucy Komisel,Otari Sakhelashvili,Anja Wachowitz*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种新的'规范轴子'（gauge axion）概念，作为QCD真空θ-项物理性的直接体现，并通过其纯规范本质避免了传统Peccei-Quinn轴子的质量等级问题；该轴子是QCD规范冗余的内在部分，以二形式场存在，其紫外完备性直接关联引力理论，并暗示基本弦的存在。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 解决强CP问题中传统Peccei-Quinn轴子面临的质量等级（quality）问题，并阐明θ-项的物理实在性。

Method: 基于QCD真空拓扑敏感度与Chern-Simons规范理论的联系，构建一种不依赖反常全局对称性的、作为QCD规范冗余一部分的二形式规范轴子，并分析其畴壁、弦结构及紫外完备性。

Result: 提出了无质量等级问题的规范轴子，证明其UV完备需引入引力理论，并推导出该轴子源必须由基本弦承载，从而建立轴子与引力/弦理论的新联系。

Conclusion: 规范轴子为强CP问题提供了更自然的解，其存在不仅阐明θ-真空的物理性，还从轴子质量保护机制出发，为基本弦和量子引力提供了独立动机。

Abstract: The topological susceptibility of the QCD vacuum provides an understanding of $θ$-vacua as vacua of a Chern-Simons gauge theory. In this way, it gives an immediate proof of the physicality of the boundary $θ$-term. This makes the essence of the strong-$CP$ puzzle very transparent and offers a solution in form of the gauge axion, which has exact quality. This axion represents an intrinsic part of the QCD gauge redundancy without any reference to an anomalous global symmetry. It is a two-form transforming under the QCD gauge symmetry. Due to its pure gauge nature, the gauge axion represents a powerful tool to monitor physics of $θ$-vacua in various regimes. Unlike the ordinary Peccei-Quinn axion, which is UV-completed into a Goldstone phase of a complex scalar and thereby suffers from the quality problem, the gauge axion is UV-completed directly into a fundamental theory of gravity. We study the domain wall and string structure of the gauge axion and show that the strings sourcing it must be a part of this fundamental theory. We thus observe that the absence of the axion quality problem motivates the presence of fundamental strings. This provides a new argument for a connection between the axion and gravity.

</details>


### [117] [Finite size effects in DBI and Born-Infeld for screened spherically symmetric objects](https://arxiv.org/abs/2512.08865)
*Jose Beltrán Jiménez,Dario Bettoni,Philippe Brax,Bert Janssen,Pablo Sampedro*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文研究了Born-Infeld电磁学和Dirac-Born-Infeld标量场理论中球对称有限尺寸物体的线性响应，发现有限尺寸效应使原本在点源近似下奇数高阶多极矩响应系数为零的特性消失，并引入偶奇多极矩间的尺度依赖层次结构，可用于通过无穷远势行为反推非线性屏蔽尺度与物体半径。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 先前工作指出点源在BI/DBI理论中奇数高阶多极响应系数为零（类似黑洞Love数消失），但实际物体具有有限尺寸，需探究其影响。

Method: 理论分析球对称有限半径物体在Born-Infeld电磁学和Dirac-Born-Infeld标量场理论中的线性响应，考察有限尺寸对多极响应系数的影响及尺度分离效应。

Result: 有限尺寸使原本为零的奇数高阶多极响应系数获得非零修正，形成由物体半径与非线性屏蔽尺度之比决定的偶奇多极矩层次结构。

Conclusion: 有限尺寸破坏了点源理想化下的奇数多极响应消失特性，该效应可作为探测非线性尺度和物体几何尺寸的可观测量。

Abstract: We study finite size effects on the linear response of spherically symmetric objects in Born-Infeld (BI) electromagnetism and Dirac-Born-Infeld (DBI) scalar field theories. Previous works show that the linear response coefficients for a point-like source vanish for odd multipoles above the dipole, a feature that resembles the vanishing of Love numbers for black holes. This work goes beyond the point-like idealisation and considers a sphere of finite radius. We find that the vanishing of the linear response coefficients ceases as they acquire a correction due to the finite size of the object. This introduces a hierarchy between the even and odd multipoles of the response coefficients determined by the separation of scales between the radius of the sphere and the screening scale of non-linearities. From a phenomenological viewpoint, the hierarchy between the odd and even multipoles would give access to the screening scale and the object's radius by measuring the behaviour of the potentials at infinity.

</details>
